Emaveni lamanyenti, utawudzinga kutsi ube nencwadzi lebuya kulesikolwa lotawufundza kuso, futsi ube nebufakazi bekutsi utawukhona kutisekela lokungenani kulomnyaka wekucala wetifundvo takho.
Hlola naleso sikhungo, kanye nemahhovisi ebantfu bekufika yalelove lofuna kucwaninga ngalo ngetimfuno letengetiwe.
Ngaphandle uma usikhulu lesimelele live, kusebenta emaveni ngalokuvamile kusho kutsi kumele ubhalise temtselo kulelive lokilo.
Umtselo ubalwa ngetindlela letingafani emaveni lahlukene, linani lemtselo liyehlukana kulelinye live nakuchatsaniswa nalelinye.
Emaveni lapho tifundza tinemandla ekutsatsa tincumo letibalulekile khona, njengeMelika neCanada, umtselo ubitwa ngekwetifundza nangekwendzawo lokuyo, ngako umtselo ungehluka sifundza ngesifundza.
